Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
	
My daughter V. Thilagavathy, aged 30 years, Who is Mentally retarded, daughter of V. Muniyammal, born on 
23rd June 1991, residing at No. 728, 9th Street, S.A. Colony, 1st Cross Street, Vyasarpadi, Chennai-600 039, shall henceforth be 
known as V. DIVYA
Chennai, 	
L.T.I.  of  V. MUNIYAMMAL
23rd August 2021.	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
(Mother)
	
S. Prabakaran, a Male child, son of Thiru T. Selvarajan, born on 8th June 1987, residing at No. 28/6 1st Street, 
Ravindran Nagar, RCC Post, Annanur, Chennai-600 109, has been living as a Trans Woman.  I have been granted Indentity 
Card No. CHN/733/2021. issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare & NMP Department, By this, 
I May be treated as a Trans Woman and shall henceforth be known as S. DEVASENA
S. PRABAKARAN
Chennai,
24th August 2021.
